# E2R Stock-Web Historical Calibration / Sector-Archetype Residual Research Round

## 0. Research Metadata

```text

price_source = Songdaiki/stock-web
stock_web_manifest_max_date = 2026-02-20
```

This loop adds **54** new R13 cross-pattern representative cases, **45** counterexamples/residual cases, and **41** current-profile residual errors for **R13 / L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC / R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM**.

R13 is the breaker panel rather than another sector room. It reuses the completed loop-14 R1~R12 historical rows and asks whether the same wiring fault appears across unrelated archetypes: headline-only Stage2 promotion, price-only 4B, late hard 4C, false Green labels, and high-MAE winners that should not be discarded when non-price evidence remains intact.

## 1. Current Calibrated Profile Assumption

```text
current_default_profile_proxy = e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated_proxy
previous_baseline_reference = e2r_2_0_baseline_reference
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = +2.0
stage3_yellow_total_min = 75.0
stage3_green_total_min = 87.0
stage3_green_revision_min = 55.0
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = +1.5
price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage = true
full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence = true
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = true
```

This file does not patch production scoring. The already-applied global axes are stress-tested, not re-proved. The proposed rows are shadow-only and scoped to the R13 cross-archetype router.

The selected R13 rows are actual trigger-level rows emitted by the R1~R12 loop-14 MDs. Each selected trigger retains `price_shard_path`, `profile_path`, `entry_date`, `entry_price`, MFE/MAE fields, corporate-action status, and `stock_web_manifest_max_date = 2026-02-20`. The atlas is raw/unadjusted; corporate-action-contaminated windows remain blocked or narrative-only.

## 13. Current Calibrated Profile Stress Test

| verdict | case_count | mechanism |
|---|---:|---|
| current_profile_false_positive | 19 | headline/price or weak evidence promoted too far |
| current_profile_correct | 13 | current proxy aligned with backtest outcome |
| current_profile_too_late | 8 | confirmation arrived after much of the move or after risk had risen |
| current_profile_missed_structural | 3 | non-price bridge existed but was not credited enough |
| current_profile_4B_too_late | 3 | non-price 4B deterioration came too late relative to drawdown |
| current_profile_too_early | 3 | watch-only evidence was treated as too actionable |
| current_profile_4C_too_late | 3 | hard thesis-break was recognized after large protection window had passed |
| current_profile_4B_too_early | 1 | local price peak risked being mistaken for full-cycle 4B |
| current_profile_data_insufficient | 1 | narrative-only or blocked window |

The current calibrated profile is directionally better than the old baseline, but loop 14 still exposes a shared residual: the system needs a router that distinguishes **evidence bridge** from **headline**, **local 4B overlay** from **full 4B**, and **hard 4C thesis break** from ordinary drawdown.

## 14. Stage2 / Yellow / Green Comparison

| item | finding |
|---|---|
| Stage2 actionable bonus | kept; but R13 recommends a cross-archetype non-price bridge before promotion from watch/headline to actionable |
| Yellow threshold 75 | kept; false-positive rows show threshold alone is insufficient without evidence-quality router |
| Green threshold 87 / revision 55 | kept/strengthened; Green should require confirmed revision or financial visibility, not a theme spike |
| green_lateness_ratio | source rows with numeric values are retained in trigger JSONL; unavailable values remain `not_applicable` |
| high-MAE survivor exception | proposed as shadow-only; high MAE should trigger review, not automatic rejection, when MFE and evidence bridge are strong |

## 15. 4B Local vs Full-window Timing Audit

| audit_item | result |
|---|---|
| 4B-related usable triggers | 21 |
| avg_four_b_local_peak_proximity | 0.83 |
| avg_four_b_full_window_peak_proximity | 0.80 |
| verdict | price-only local peaks should stay as overlay-only unless valuation, revision slowdown, dilution/CB, legal block, margin slowdown, or other non-price evidence confirms full 4B |

## 16. 4C Protection Audit

| audit_item | result |
|---|---|
| 4C-related usable triggers | 10 |
| hard_4c_success / hard_4c_late labels | retained from source trigger rows; R13 does not invent new 4C timing labels |
| verdict | 4C should be routed only when thesis evidence breaks: cancellation, regulatory rejection, safety/trial failure, accounting/trust break, forced liquidation, or explicit thesis evidence broken |

## 18. Canonical-Archetype Rule Candidate

```text
canonical_archetype_rule_candidate = true
rule_scope = R13_cross_archetype_shadow_router
new_axis_proposed = NON_PRICE_BRIDGE_REQUIRED_FOR_POSITIVE_STAGE | LOCAL_4B_OVERLAY_NOT_FULL_EXIT | HARD_4C_THESIS_BREAK_ROUTER | HIGH_MAE_STRUCTURAL_SURVIVOR_EXCEPTION
existing_axis_strengthened = price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage | full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence | hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c
existing_axis_weakened = null
```

## 26. Deferred Coding Agent Handoff Prompt

### Purpose

You are now in the repository implementation phase. The attached Markdown files are v12 post-calibrated residual research outputs produced using the Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC atlas.

These MDs are not live candidate research. They are historical calibration research designed to extend the already-applied e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated profile.

Do not blindly apply every shadow row. Ingest the machine-readable rows and update the sector/canonical-archetype calibration ledger.

### Price source context

- Primary historical price source used by the research MD: Songdaiki/stock-web.
- Price basis: tradable_raw.
- Price adjustment status: raw_unadjusted_marcap.
- Price shard pattern: atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year/<prefix>/<ticker>/<year>.csv.
- Symbol profile pattern: atlas/symbol_profiles/<prefix>/<ticker>.json.

### Rules

- Use only calibration_usable=true rows for quantitative calibration.
- Do not count reused cases as new independent evidence unless independent_evidence_weight > 0.
- Do not treat schema_rematerialization_only or duplicate_low_value_loop as new evidence.
- Do not apply global deltas unless multiple large_sector_id values support the same direction.
- Prefer sector_specific or canonical_archetype_specific shadow profiles.
- Positive score promotion requires non-price evidence and clean 180D MFE/MAE.
- 4B rows are overlay/risk calibration only.
- 4C rows are thesis-break/protection calibration only.
- price-only rows cannot promote Stage2/Stage3.
- If a v12 MD weakens an already applied axis, log it as residual counterexample rather than immediately reverting.
- Production scoring must not change unless the user explicitly asks for another promotion batch.

### Expected repository tasks

1. Parse case / trigger / score_simulation / shadow_weight / residual_contribution rows.
2. Validate stock-web price source fields.
3. Validate large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
4. Validate novelty and reuse fields.
5. Deduplicate same_entry_group_id and reused cases.
6. Aggregate by large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
7. Update sector_shadow_profile and archetype_shadow_profile only.
8. Preserve global calibrated profile unless explicitly promoted.
9. Report new independent cases, counterexamples, and residual error types.
10. Add tests that duplicate low-value loops cannot change weights.

### Expected output

- Concise implementation summary.
- Rows accepted/rejected.
- New sector/canonical archetype coverage.
- Existing axis strengthened/weakened/kept.
- No investment recommendation language.

- Stock-Web manifest was checked in this run. The manifest reports `max_date = 2026-02-20`, `price_adjustment_status = raw_unadjusted_marcap`, and calibration shard root `atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year`.
- Stock-Web schema was checked in this run. It defines tradable shard columns `d,o,h,l,c,v,a,mc,s,m` and the MFE/MAE formulas used by the source rows.
- All case/trigger rows in this R13 file are transformed from local loop-14 R1~R12 source MD machine-readable rows. They preserve the source stock-web price fields and metrics.
- This is not an investment recommendation, not a live watchlist, and not a stock_agent code patch.
